select A.id,A.goods_id,A.user_id,A.thematic_id,A.record_id,A.status,A.code,A.add_time,B.goods_sn,B.goods_title,B.price,B.goods_thumb,B.free_post,C.thematic_name,D.nickname,D.user_img,D.phone from bill as A  left join goods as B on A.goods_id=B.id left join thematic as C on A.thematic_id=C.id left join user as D on A.user_id=D.id where A.is_on=1 and A.is_confirm=1 and A.goods_id=43
